[?2004l]3008;start=72462a9e-a831-42f4-8334-e042516fa022;machineid=69c4c6fade2c4aa683f39b0f0eb549cf;user=ras;hostname=fedora;bootid=98e532df-ab17-47ea-a681-5a8790780935;pid=00000000000000006085;type=command;cwd=/home/ras/linux/week03/web_service/html\Usage: useradd [options] LOGIN
       useradd -D
       useradd -D [options]

Options:
      --badname                 do not check for bad names
  -b, --base-dir BASE_DIR       base directory for the home directory of the
                                new account
      --btrfs-subvolume-home    use BTRFS subvolume for home directory
  -c, --comment COMMENT         GECOS field of the new account
  -d, --home-dir HOME_DIR       home directory of the new account
  -D, --defaults                print or change default useradd configuration
  -e, --expiredate EXPIRE_DATE  expiration date of the new account
  -f, --inactive INACTIVE       password inactivity period of the new account
  -F, --add-subids-for-system   add entries to sub[ud]id even when adding a system user
  -g, --gid GROUP               name or ID of the primary group of the new
                                account
  -G, --groups GROUPS           list of supplementary groups of the new
                                account
  -h, --help                    display this help message and exit
  -k, --skel SKEL_DIR           use this alternative skeleton directory
  -K, --key KEY=VALUE           override /etc/login.defs defaults
  -m, --create-home             create the user's home directory
  -M, --no-create-home          do not create the user's home directory
  -N, --no-user-group           do not create a group with the same name as
                                the user
  -o, --non-unique              allow to create users with duplicate
                                (non-unique) UID
  -p, --password PASSWORD       encrypted password of the new account
  -r, --system                  create a system account
  -R, --root CHROOT_DIR         directory to chroot into
  -P, --prefix PREFIX_DIR       prefix directory where are located the /etc/* files
  -s, --shell SHELL             login shell of the new account
  -u, --uid UID                 user ID of the new account
  -U, --user-group              create a group with the same name as the user
  -Z, --selinux-user SEUSER     use a specific SEUSER for the SELinux user mapping
      --selinux-range SERANGE   use a specific MLS range for the SELinux user mapping

[1;43r[40;1H[36m# Cmnd_Alias PROCESSES = /bin/nice, /bin/kill, /usr/bin/kill, /usr/bin/killall[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d

[1;43r[40;1H[36m# Defaults specification[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# Refuse to run if unable to disable echo on the tty.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults   !visiblepw[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# Preserving HOME has security implications since many programs[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# use it when searching for configuration files. Note that HOME[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# is already set when the the env_reset option is enabled, so[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# this option is only effective for configurations where either[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# env_reset is disabled or HOME is present in the env_keep list.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults    always_set_home[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults    match_group_by_gid[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# Prior to version 1.8.15, groups listed in sudoers that were not[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# found in the system group database were passed to the group[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# plugin, if any. Starting with 1.8.15, only groups of the form[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# %:group are resolved via the group plugin by default.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# We enable always_query_group_plugin to restore old behavior.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# Disable this option for new behavior.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults    always_query_group_plugin[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults    env_reset[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults    env_keep =  "COLORS DISPLAY HOSTNAME HISTSIZE KDEDIR LS_COLORS"[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults    env_keep += "MAIL QTDIR USERNAME LANG LC_ADDRESS LC_CTYPE"[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults    env_keep += "LC_COLLATE LC_IDENTIFICATION LC_MEASUREMENT LC_MESSAGES"[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults    env_keep += "LC_MONETARY LC_NAME LC_NUMERIC LC_PAPER LC_TELEPHONE"[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1HDefaults    env_keep += "LC_TIME LC_ALL LANGUAGE LINGUAS _XKB_CHARSET XAUTHORITY"[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# Adding HOME to env_keep may enable a user to run unrestricted[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d

[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## Next comes the main part: which users can run what software on [39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## which machines (the sudoers file can be shared between multiple[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## systems).[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## Syntax:[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m##[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## [38;5;208m     [36muser[38;5;208m    [36mMACHINE=COMMANDS[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m##[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## The COMMANDS section may have other options added to it.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m##[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## Allow root to run any commands anywhere [39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1Hroot[38;5;208m    [39m(B[mALL=(ALL)[41m [49m[38;5;208m      [39m(B[mALL[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## Allows members of the 'sys' group to run networking, software, [39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## service management apps and more.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# %sys ALL = NETWORKING, SOFTWARE, SERVICES, STORAGE, DELEGATING, PROCESSES, LOCATE, DRIVERS[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## Allows people in group wheel to run all commands[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H%wheel[38;5;208m  [39m(B[mALL=(ALL)[38;5;208m       [39m(B[mALL[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## Same thing without a password[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# %wheel[38;5;208m        [36mALL=(ALL)[38;5;208m       [36mNOPASSWD: ALL[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## Allows members of the users group to mount and unmount the [39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## cdrom as root[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# %users  ALL=/sbin/mount /mnt/cdrom, /sbin/umount /mnt/cdrom[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## Allows members of the users group to shutdown this system[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m# %users  localhost=/sbin/shutdown -h now[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m## Read drop-in files from /etc/sudoers.d (the # here does not mean a comment)[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d
[1;43r[40;1H[36m#includedir /etc/sudoers.d[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;41r8[41d

로컬 시스템 관리자에게 일반적인 지침을 받았으리라 믿습니다.
보통 세가지로 요약합니다:

    #1) 타인의 사생활을 존중하십시오.
    #2) 입력하기 전에 한 번 더 생각하십시오.
    #3) 막강한 힘에는 상당한 책임이 뒤따릅니다.

보안상 사유로, 입력한 암호는 나타나지 않습니다.

[sudo] web-admin 암호: 
web-admin은(는) sudoers 파일에 없습니다.

# Source global definitions
if [ -f /etc/bashrc ]; then
    . /etc/bashrc
fi

# User specific environment
if ! [[ "$PATH" =~ "$HOME/.local/bin:$HOME/bin:" ]]; then
    PATH="$HOME/.local/bin:$HOME/bin:$PATH"
fi
export PATH

# Uncomment the following line if you don't like systemctl's auto-paging feature:
# export SYSTEMD_PAGER=

# User specific aliases and functions
if [ -d ~/.bashrc.d ]; then
    for rc in ~/.bashrc.d/*; do
        if [ -f "$rc" ]; then
            . "$rc"
        fi
    done
fi
unset rc
]0;root@fedora:/etc/skel]3008;end=32bb61b2-a99b-468c-b1eb-f95fbc571eee;exit=success\]3008;start=11773bfc-82ca-4bbc-9a9e-8addd2b1236f;machineid=69c4c6fade2c4aa683f39b0f0eb549cf;user=root;hostname=fedora;bootid=98e532df-ab17-47ea-a681-5a8790780935;pid=00000000000000034462;type=shell;cwd=/etc/skel\[?2004h[0m[35mroot@fedora[0m:[35m/etc/skel[0m# cat /etc/bashrc

# System wide functions and aliases
# Environment stuff goes in /etc/profile

# It's NOT a good idea to change this file unless you know what you
# are doing. It's much better to create a custom.sh shell script in
# /etc/profile.d/ to make custom changes to your environment, as this
# will prevent the need for merging in future updates.

# Prevent doublesourcing
if [ -z "$BASHRCSOURCED" ]; then
  BASHRCSOURCED="Y"

  # are we an interactive shell?
  if [ "$PS1" ]; then
    if [ -z "$PROMPT_COMMAND" ]; then
      declare -a PROMPT_COMMAND
      case $TERM in
      xterm*)
        if [ -e /etc/sysconfig/bash-prompt-xterm ]; then
            PROMPT_COMMAND=/etc/sysconfig/bash-prompt-xterm
        else
            PROMPT_COMMAND='printf "\033]0;%s@%s:%s\007" "${USER}" "${HOSTNAME%%.*}" "${PWD/#$HOME/\~}"'
        fi
        ;;
      screen*)
        if [ -e /etc/sysconfig/bash-prompt-screen ]; then
            PROMPT_COMMAND=/etc/sysconfig/bash-prompt-screen
        else
            PROMPT_COMMAND='printf "\033k%s@%s:%s\033\\" "${USER}" "${HOSTNAME%%.*}" "${PWD/#$HOME/\~}"'
        fi
        ;;
      *)
        [ -e /etc/sysconfig/bash-prompt-default ] && PROMPT_COMMAND=/etc/sysconfig/bash-prompt-default
        ;;
      esac
    fi
    # Turn on parallel history
    shopt -s histappend
    # Turn on checkwinsize
    shopt -s checkwinsize
    # Change the default prompt string
    [ "$PS1" = "\\s-\\v\\\$ " ] && PS1="[\u@\h \W]\\$ "
    # You might want to have e.g. tty in prompt (e.g. more virtual machines)
    # and console windows
    # If you want to do so, just add e.g.
    # if [ "$PS1" ]; then
    #   PS1="[\u@\h:\l \W]\\$ "
    # fi
    # to your custom modification shell script in /etc/profile.d/ directory
  fi

  if ! shopt -q login_shell ; then # We're not a login shell
    # Need to redefine pathmunge, it gets undefined at the end of /etc/profile
    pathmunge () {
        case ":${PATH}:" in
            *:"$1":*)
                ;;
            *)
                if [ "$2" = "after" ] ; then
                    PATH=$PATH:$1
                else
                    PATH=$1:$PATH
                fi
        esac
    }

    # Set default umask for non-login shell only if it is set to 0
    [ `umask` -eq 0 ] && umask 022

    SHELL=/bin/bash
    # Only display echos from profile.d scripts if we are no login shell
    # and interactive - otherwise just process them to set envvars
    for i in /etc/profile.d/*.sh; do
        if [ -r "$i" ]; then
            if [ "$PS1" ]; then
                . "$i"
            else
                . "$i" >/dev/null
            fi
        fi
    done

    unset i
    unset -f pathmunge
  fi

fi

]0;root@fedora:/etc/skel]3008;end=e557e6f9-32fb-4114-92c4-0d47aaecaa4f;exit=success\]3008;start=11773bfc-82ca-4bbc-9a9e-8addd2b1236f;machineid=69c4c6fade2c4aa683f39b0f0eb549cf;user=root;hostname=fedora;bootid=98e532df-ab17-47ea-a681-5a8790780935;pid=00000000000000034462;type=shell;cwd=/etc/skel\[?2004h[0m[35mroot@fedora[0m:[35m/etc/skel[0m# cat /etc/bashrc | more[K[K[K[K[K[K[K[K[K[K[K[K[Kprofile
[?2004l]3008;start=bbdb6277-f341-473a-813b-e1a9b69b67a3;machineid=69c4c6fade2c4aa683f39b0f0eb549cf;user=root;hostname=fedora;bootid=98e532df-ab17-47ea-a681-5a8790780935;pid=00000000000000034462;type=command;cwd=/etc/skel\# /etc/profile

# System wide environment and startup programs, for login setup
# Functions and aliases go in /etc/bashrc

# It's NOT a good idea to change this file unless you know what you
# are doing. It's much better to create a custom.sh shell script in
# /etc/profile.d/ to make custom changes to your environment, as this
# will prevent the need for merging in future updates.

pathmunge () {
    # If the path is a compat symlink, do nothing.
    [ -h "$1" ] && return

    case ":${PATH}:" in
        *:"$1":*)
            ;;
        *)
            if [ "$2" = "after" ] ; then
                PATH=$PATH:$1
            else
                PATH=$1:$PATH
            fi
    esac
}


if [ -x /usr/bin/id ]; then
    if [ -z "$EUID" ]; then
        # ksh workaround
        EUID=`/usr/bin/id -u`
        UID=`/usr/bin/id -ru`
    fi
    USER="`/usr/bin/id -un`"
    LOGNAME=$USER
    MAIL="/var/spool/mail/$USER"
fi

# Path manipulation
if [ "$EUID" = "0" ]; then
    pathmunge /usr/sbin
    pathmunge /usr/local/sbin
else
    pathmunge /usr/local/sbin after
    pathmunge /usr/sbin after
fi

HOSTNAME=$(/usr/bin/hostnamectl --transient 2>/dev/null) || \
HOSTNAME=$(/usr/bin/hostname 2>/dev/null) || \
HOSTNAME=$(/usr/bin/uname -n)

if [ -z "$HISTSIZE" ] ; then
    HISTSIZE=1000
fi

if [ "$HISTCONTROL" = "ignorespace" ] ; then
    export HISTCONTROL=ignoreboth
else
    export HISTCONTROL=ignoredups
fi

export PATH USER LOGNAME MAIL HOSTNAME HISTSIZE HISTCONTROL

    if [ -r "$i" ]; then
        if [ "${-#*i}" != "$-" ]; then
            . "$i"
        else
            . "$i" >/dev/null
        fi
    fi
done

   test "${0#-}" != sh &&\
   test -r /etc/bashrc
then
   # Bash login shells run only /etc/profile
   # Bash non-login shells run only /etc/bashrc
   # Check for double sourcing is done in /etc/bashrc.
   . /etc/bashrc
fi

[?2004l]3008;start=cbcbea42-df83-44a9-b48e-b1f396fb3d49;machineid=69c4c6fade2c4aa683f39b0f0eb549cf;user=root;hostname=fedora;bootid=98e532df-ab17-47ea-a681-5a8790780935;pid=00000000000000034462;type=command;cwd=/etc/skel\# /etc/profile

# System wide environment and startup programs, for login setup
# Functions and aliases go in /etc/bashrc

# It's NOT a good idea to change this file unless you know what you
# are doing. It's much better to create a custom.sh shell script in
# /etc/profile.d/ to make custom changes to your environment, as this
# will prevent the need for merging in future updates.

pathmunge () {
    # If the path is a compat symlink, do nothing.
    [ -h "$1" ] && return

    case ":${PATH}:" in
        *:"$1":*)
            ;;
        *)
            if [ "$2" = "after" ] ; then
                PATH=$PATH:$1
            else
                PATH=$1:$PATH
            fi
    esac
}


if [ -x /usr/bin/id ]; then
    if [ -z "$EUID" ]; then
        # ksh workaround
        EUID=`/usr/bin/id -u`
        UID=`/usr/bin/id -ru`
    fi
    USER="`/usr/bin/id -un`"
    LOGNAME=$USER
    MAIL="/var/spool/mail/$USER"
fi

# Path manipulation
if [ "$EUID" = "0" ]; then
    pathmunge /usr/sbin
    pathmunge /usr/local/sbin
[7m--More--[27melse[K
    pathmunge /usr/local/sbin after
    pathmunge /usr/sbin after
fi

HOSTNAME=$(/usr/bin/hostnamectl --transient 2>/dev/null) || \
HOSTNAME=$(/usr/bin/hostname 2>/dev/null) || \
HOSTNAME=$(/usr/bin/uname -n)

if [ -z "$HISTSIZE" ] ; then
    HISTSIZE=1000
fi

if [ "$HISTCONTROL" = "ignorespace" ] ; then
    export HISTCONTROL=ignoreboth
else
    export HISTCONTROL=ignoredups
fi

export PATH USER LOGNAME MAIL HOSTNAME HISTSIZE HISTCONTROL

for i in /etc/profile.d/*.sh /etc/profile.d/sh.local ; do
    if [ -r "$i" ]; then
        if [ "${-#*i}" != "$-" ]; then
            . "$i"
        else
            . "$i" >/dev/null
        fi
    fi
done

unset i
unset -f pathmunge

# Source global bash config, when interactive but not posix or sh mode
if test "$BASH" &&\
   test -z "$POSIXLY_CORRECT" &&\
   test "${0#-}" != sh &&\
   test -r /etc/bashrc
then
   # Bash login shells run only /etc/profile
   # Bash non-login shells run only /etc/bashrc
[7m--More--[27m   # Check for double sourcing is done in /etc/bashrc.
   . /etc/bashrc
fi
